## Quality Re-Audit Baseline

Fresh read-only headless export on 2026-05-13 shows the next campaign should optimize for confidence, not just name coverage.

| Metric | Value | Source |
|--------|------:|--------|

| Legacy weak names (`FUN_`, `Auto_`, `__Unk_`) | 0 | `tools/ghidra_static_reaudit_baseline_probe.py --check` |
| Broad uncertain owner names (`_Unk_` style) | 0 | same probe |
| Address-suffixed helper names | 0 | same probe |
| Address-suffixed wrapper names | 0 | same probe |
| Signatures still using `param_N` names | 1980 | same probe |
| `undefined` signatures | 1939 | same probe |
| Seed missing function objects | `<none>` | same probe |

Interpretation:

- `weak-name objects = 0` means the legacy weak-regex backlog is closed.
- It does not mean every name, owner, signature, comment, tag, or boundary is correct.
- The next static RE campaign should grade every function by evidence class, then refine names/signatures/comments/tags in small dry-run/read-back tranches.
- The current weapon/burst cluster is the first explicit re-audit seed because its current names are useful labels but not settled source identities.

This queue snapshot is the current whole-database triage surface after the Wave435 CMCTentacle / CMCWarspiteDome correction tranche and all earlier saved-Ghidra tranches. It does not mean the currently commented functions are complete or correct; comments, names, signatures, boundaries, and future tags still need evidence-grade review in small tranches.

Wave435 is the latest saved-Ghidra hardening tranche on this queue. It hardens eighteen `CMCTentacle` / `CMCWarspiteDome` targets after Wave434 handled the neighboring `CMCMine` / `CMCSentinel` cluster. The pass creates four missing vtable-slot boundaries, corrects stale tentacle mesh-filter labels, and keeps runtime motion behavior deferred. It does not make the long queue paragraph above complete or final.

Current proxy answer for "how far are we in 100% confirmation": the broad comment-backed proxy is `1791 / 6055 = 29.58%`; the stricter comment-plus-no-`undefined`-or-`param_N` proxy is `1729 / 6055 = 28.55%`. These are triage proxies, not certification, and crossing any round number by either proxy is not a milestone or completion gate; the target remains as close to `100%` evidence-grade RE as possible.

## Stuart-Source Mappable Corpus Coverage

| Metric | Value | Source |
|--------|-------|--------|
| Source-file entries tracked | 160 | Count of numeric `Functions` table rows in [`_index.md`](./_index.md) |

| Source-file directories with index | 137 | `functions/<source-file>/_index.md` folders |

## Interpretation

- Binary-wide `% mapped` is measured against all Ghidra function objects (includes runtime helpers, thunks, compiler helpers, and code not present in Stuart debug-path corpus).
- Stuart-source corpus totals are a separate axis: they measure source-aligned coverage, not total executable coverage.
- A function being "named" does not automatically mean "fully verified"; verification still depends on owner, boundary, signature, comment, tag, doc, and source/runtime evidence quality.
- `weak-name` is a narrow regex metric (`FUN_`, `Auto_`, `__Unk_`). Helper placeholders (`__Helper_`) are tracked separately; that backlog is now closed in `pass2_semantic_wave217`.
